           *1 to 5*
 
 *KAMAL...*

Kwance yake kan resting chair dake by d swimming pool syd ya d'ora  hannunsa akarkashen k'ansa  staring at d cloudy sky ..iska ke kad'awa mae sanyi soosae hkn yasa flowers  n trees na kad'awa .

eye brow din shi kmar ya yi carving ,looking extra ordinary black ..his nose is soo pointed har a baki ,and gashin kanshi bak'i ne da ratsen golden brown aciki ,anyi curling d'inshi  sae uban shinning dayakeyi waye an zube bottle of oil akai

✨•✨•✨•✨•✨•✨✨✨

     Fans d'ina kunsan gu junpyoo na ckin boys before flowers?... zaku CE shi ne wlhy sadae yapi shi kyau nesa ba kusa ba...d guy is soo breath takingly beautiful😘😘..


     He's d only son to his multi billonaire father senator AYDIN sayeed..who owns an edge of paradise company called *KINGDOM*.... 
 

    A company d'in ba abinda baa  producing.kmar su bags,shoes, clothes,jeweries ,chocolate, biscuits, candies ,food items kae everything ma....
 
  
     phone dinshi dake by d Syd table tayi ringing ...guards din dake behind him suka dauko su bashi..
*iPhone 7*ce gold plated yaduba ya ga best frnd dinshi k kira Wanda hkan ya sanya shi smiling dimples inshi suka yi appearing sae da wyt teeth dinshi wadanda  kmar annyi leveling dinsu suka fito ...wow Allah his smiles 
kills  



       ya d'aga  wayar ckin wani honey voice dinshi da "hy dude ,d oda Lyn frnd dinshi yace hi *HANDSOME* aw av u bn doing (zakuyi mamakin namiji da kiran shi *HANDSOME* bt hka kowa k cemasa both boys n gals men da women young and old ..)  
 
    
🎇✨🎇✨🎇✨🎇✨🎇

Luckily to her yau yayi bacci lokacin tak'are 4 chapters zata shiga ta Biyar ...ya ye transparent curtains d'in tayi ta lek'a dan ta tabbatar yayi bacci...he was sleeping heavily kuwa..fuskarshi ta kalla Kan tace aranta " hmm ance _the devil sleeps peacefully_  amma banda wannan see his smirked faced still clearly seen,nan ta tashi ta tafi ...
_washe gari_
     Bayan ta had'a breakfast taje tayi wanka ta shirya cikin Pakistan d'inta lime colour ...tayi kyau soosae , tayi serving nasu _mince meat pie _ ne da _egg drop soup_  
Bayan suntafi ayki ta bud'e su zara su kayi breakfast suka shiga gyran gida...d'akin kamal take gyra mistakely, ta buge wani  _glass porcelain_ cylinder shape ne  Wanda zae kae tsawon ta , ya fashe tas cikin d'akin,   jikin ta ya shiga b'ari kasancewar tasan Kamal na bala'in so nae dan yadda take gani yana admiring d'inshi...unknown to her gift d'in da dad d'inshi yabashi ne on his 18th birthday, dan hadda pic d'inshi da na dad d'inshi aka yi designing kan _glass porcelain_  d'in, gashi kuma sunyi kyau soosae...daga ni zakasan at a high cost akayi shi...   K'ara soosae tasaki wanda yasa zara tabar ironing d'in da takeyi ta iso duba ta...itama ta tsorata, jikinsu Yamutu suna tsoron hukunci da zae yanke in yadawo...ilhaam ta iske su d'akin  tare da fad' in " ya zara!!! Kayan mister sun k'one  !! Sae alokacin zara ta tuna da tabar iron kunne tana goge  sweat wears (shirts da trousers na shan iska) d'in kamal........

_@ 12: 50_
Minal ta dawo daga wurin koyon girki tashiga kitchen ta dafa lunch, nan ta wuce d'aki  ta tarad dasu zara. sukayi sallah San nan suka ci..lunch.
Kamal sun dawo  daga office , straight d'aki ya nufa, ga serious headache d'in da  ke damunsa yasa bae lura _glass porcelain_ d'in shi bata wurin da take , bathroom yashiga yayi taking shower ya dawo d'aki d'aure da towel a waist nashi, sae Lokacin ya lura bae ga _preciouus porcelain_ gabanshi ya pad'i yana tunanin ina take nan har zae kira minal dan yasan ita kad'ae ke gyra d'akin, ya tuna da ba kaya jikinshi ,  k'ofar  dressing room d'in da ke cikin d'akinshi ya nufa.. Na d'akin su minal, yau tun da ta dawo jikinta a sanyayye dan tasan laefin da ta aykata yau..zaune take ta zuba uban tagumi jin k'ara telephone ta tashi da Sauri ta d'aga wayar, ko gaeda shi batae ba yace da ita " come to my room now!" Ya katse wayar..jikinta a sanyaye , zara sae encouraging nata take yi dak'yar ta tafi.

Kan couch ta sa meshi zaune yayi crossing leg..sadda kanta k'asa tayi kan tace "good after..." "Am talking to a deaf living being ne"?  .d'ago kae tayi idonta sae hawaye ke fitowa kamar rainfall, " am...so...rry ..sir ...wlhy ...acciden...ta..lly ya ...fashe..."idonshi ya zaroo sosae,  Kan kamal ya Gaza d'aukar abinda yaji ..watau ta halaka Mae da precious possession d'insa dayake Mutuwar so! Lallae yarinyar nan ta ja Mae babbar hasara ...mi ta ke nufi he av to teach her a lesson,..." Oh Allah Hafiz ! Who the hell are you ...shi precious possession d'in nawa kika fasa?.....ya pad'a atsawace..minal tayi kneeling tana kuka tace " ka yafe pls, bawanda ya wuce k'addara..Amman nama alk'awarin zan yi ma same exact one iri  ne.." K'atseta yayi da cewa " will you shutup ! Angayamiki zaki Iya biya na shi..ko salaryn ki 10× bazae saye shi ba, limited edition mutum biyu aka ma iri nae the whole world wide @ U.S 7 yrs back abbana yaba nashi, amma since zaki Iya biya , I will be deducting 200,000 thousands from your salary sae in rink'a baki 50k d'in da suka yi saura  har ki biya shi ...kuma kinsan ba wae banida kud'i bane , you knw that am one of the richest youngman in africa, but that will be a lesson for you!.... " haka ya rink'a masifeta kamar an ayko shi ....minal tun da ya fara kuka takae kanta a k'asa...yau siraj bae kusa bare yayi saving d'inta...
Asanyaye ta sauko Stairs tana tunanin dream d'inta na making siblings d'inta educated bazae zama real ba ...d'aki ta koma tana kuka .. Daky'ar ta Iya bawa zara labarin hukuncin da ya yanke mata .. _3 dayys later_

As usual ta gama dinner ta shirya zata tafi wurin ayki kasancewar yau su Kamal  ko lunch basu dawo yi ba dan sunce yau suna da upcoming project dasu keyi sae dare zasu dawo, hakan yasa minal taji daad'i dan tasan yau basu yini gida ba, kuma bazasu dawo da wuri ba , soo k'ila sae  gobe zae kore siblings nata duk tana da Niyyar rik'onshi ya k'ara musu kwanaki..nan ta shirya ta fice bayan tayi sallama dasu zara...

Rikicewa siraj yayi ganin minal, shi kuwa Kamal yana kan wayarsa yana pressing, dak'arfi minal ta k'wace kanta ta ruga sae jikin siraj tayi hugging nashi gam, dan masifar tsoro da tashin hankalin  da taji ganin abinda zayd zae yimita , kuka takeyi kamar an aykota tana fad'in " _yaa.... siraj... pls... save... me, pls ...save ....me.. from... this ...evil man, dan ...Allah ..yaa siraj ka cece ni ...kar ...ka bari ...ya min ko mae...u're are my..  gurdian... angel ...you came ....the right time ...I need you...pls save..me_  tak'are maganar tana hugging nashi tighter...Kamal shi kanshi ba karamin rud'ewa yayi ba ganin avinda ke faruwa, brain d'in siraj gaba d'aya tayi hooking yana mamakin meke faruwa da Angel , consoling nata yafara yi yana shafar kanta yana Cewa " nothing will happen to you angel am right here by your side I will save you..." k'ara rud'ewa siraj yayi ganinta ta uniform d'in waitress...haka dae ya daure ya d'ago kae yana kallon Mr.zayd evily...minal kuwa kuka kawae takeyi, Nan siraj ya d'agota suka mik'e, veil nata da ke k'asa ya d'akko ya mayar mata akanta  ya ja hannunta suka fita *bar* d'in, kowa wurin kallon abinda yafaru yakeyi da mamaki...mota siraj yakae minal ya sata ciki..yace da ita tabari yazo , amma ina kuka kwae takeyi wae za su dawo sumaida ta ciki in yatafi ya barta ,rarrashinta yashiga yi  dak'yar ta yadda yatafi..komawa yayi cikin bar d'in , Managern wurin kekira nae , wae who is he da zae yimusu haka...Mr. Zayd kuwa ya wani had'e rae adole sae anmaida Mae da  minal ...aykuwa wurin managern siraj ta tafi straight, da rawar jiki managern ya tarbe shi ganin siraj kasancewar he's well known, him being the bestfriend of kamal sole heir of *KINGDOM* ....
Kud'i masu yawa siraj ya zuba masa ya fice, yace da Kamal yasame shi gida, Kamal ko ransa ya b'ace ya zae wuce ya barshi wurin bayan yasan sunada appointment dawani .
Siraj Mota yakoma ya iske minal na aykin kuka ...consoling nata yayi tayi har ta daena kuka, kan yashiga tambayarta mi yafaru?


Magana tafara tana hawaye " ya siraj ...nasab'a ..ma
. Allah, na ...butulce mishi ...sae yanxu nayi danasanin aykin nan Dana fara..yaa siraaj in baka manta ba yau ne Mr Kamal yace siblings d'ina su barmae gida..banda kud'in da zan sami haya (hire) , kuma dole tare dasu zan bar gidan , in muka bar gidan sae mun nema abinci, ga kud'i transport d'ina zuwa gidan, gashi yace sae yayi deducting salaryn na ...." Haka minal tabashi labarin yadda sukayi about his _glass porcelain_ d'in da ta fasa, da salaryn ta da yace zae rage ,da dae-dae matsalolin da zasuyi facing insuka bar gidan har ta nemi ayki, har haka ta faru ...tabashi labarin komae, ta k'ara ba siraj tausayi, yaji haushin abinda Kamal yayi mata duk da yasan wasa yakeyi he is just testing her, dan yasan Kamal bazae cire kud'in ba cemata kawae ne yayi...minal tacigaba tana hawaye "kaga siraj na butulce ma Allah, dan shi da ya taimake mu farko, ko yanzu shi zae taemake mu , amma naje Ina ayki agidan giya..." Why ?..minal ta katse shi cikin kuka atsawace dacewa " yaa siraj because i'm only thinking of a way to SURVIVE ..!!" Siraj ma atsawace yace da ita " to Miyasa baki fad'amin min ba , kinsan I will not leave you in this mess?? A sanyaye minal tayi k'asa da murya tace " yaa siraj saboda ko yanzu abinda kayi min kad'ae ya isa haka, dan nasan akan kawae bae koreni ba har yanxu , kuma naga  wlhy da nauyi in tambaye ka wani abu bayan abinda kamin ..." Ta fashe da wani matsanancin kuka da yabawa siraj tausae , dak'yar tace " kaga siraj na sab'a ma ubangijina , yanzu ....ga... irinta,na ..butulce masa" nan ta d'aga hannu sama tana rok'on Allah gafara... hawaye takeyi kamar rainfall tana fad'in "ya ..ubangijini ka yafe ni..." Ya tafi office yasame  ummanshi bakin k'ofar office tana jiranshi, nan ta cimae mutunci , Kuma ta tabbatar Mae da aurenshi da meera dole , ko yaso ko kar  yaso k'arshen satin nan, Kuma tana tabbatar Mae dacewa shima bae fi k'arfin ta asirce shi ba...
